A copy of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information contained in Item 2.02 of this report and Exhibit 99.1 attached hereto shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section, nor shall it be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

with break-even results in the prior year&#146;s second quarter </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Excluding CARES Act benefits, Adjusted EBITDA of $2.6&nbsp;million or 8.7% or revenue </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Company anticipates sequential and year-over-year <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-line</FONT> growth in the
second half of fiscal 2022 </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>West Warwick, R.I. &#150; September</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;14, 2021</B> &#150; AstroNova, Inc. (NASDAQ:
ALOT), a global leader in data visualization technologies, today announced financial results for the fiscal 2022 second quarter ended July&nbsp;31, 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>CEO Commentary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We reported year-over-year
and sequential revenue growth in the second quarter in both the Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement and Product Identification segments, as we capitalized on an improved demand picture across the business,&#148; said Gregory A. Woods, President and Chief
Executive Officer of AstroNova. &#147;In the Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement segment, revenue from hardware, supplies, and parts and repairs all increased as air passenger traffic continued to rebound. We also saw solid contributions across the Product
Identification product line, with another strong quarter from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T3-OPX</FONT> wide-format durable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">direct-to-package</FONT></FONT> printing system.
We performed particularly well given the ongoing global supply chain constraints and continuing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> headwinds.&#148; </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Business Outlook </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We expect to report year-over-year and sequential <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-line</FONT> growth for the second half of fiscal 2022,&#148;
continued Woods. &#147;The aerospace market is recovering a bit more quickly than we had anticipated, and we expect continued improved demand in the Product Identification segment. At the same time, we recognize the uncertainty caused by supply
chain constraints and the continuing pandemic. Looking further ahead, we believe that we are well positioned to capitalize on many growth opportunities across both our Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement and Product Identification segments when markets
fully recover.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>CARES Act Benefits </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the second quarter of this fiscal year, the principal and interest were forgiven on the Paycheck Protection Program (PPP) loan AstroNova received last
year. In addition, the Company became eligible for an Employee Retention Credit (ERC) authorized under the Coronavirus Aid, Relief, and Economic Security (CARES) Act. In total for the second quarter, these two items (the CARES Act benefits)
benefited net income by $6.0&nbsp;million and earnings per diluted share by $0.83. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Q2 FY 2022 Operating Segment Results </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Product Identification</B> segment revenue in the second quarter of fiscal 2022 increased 8.6% to $23.5&nbsp;million, with gains in both hardware and
supplies, versus $21.6&nbsp;million in the prior-year period. GAAP segment operating income was $4.4&nbsp;million, or 18.8% of revenue, compared with $3.1&nbsp;million, or 14.5% of revenue, in the prior year. On a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis, excluding the CARES Act benefits, segment operating income in the second quarter of fiscal 2022 was $3.0&nbsp;million, or 12.7% of revenue. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Test</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;&amp; Measurement </B>segment revenue in the second quarter of fiscal 2022 was $6.4&nbsp;million, compared with $6.0&nbsp;million
in the same period of fiscal 2021. The Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement segment recorded GAAP operating income of $1.7&nbsp;million, or 26.9% of revenue, compared with a segment operating loss of $0.4&nbsp;million, or negative 6.8% of revenue, in the
comparable period of fiscal 2021. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> segment operating income in the second quarter of fiscal 2022, excluding the CARES Act benefits, was $908,000, or 14.3% of sales, helped by lower manufacturing costs
and operating expenses versus the year-earlier period, as well as a change in amortization for aerospace-related intangibles that resulted in an additional $587,000 in operating profit. This is the best result since the second half of fiscal 2020,
when revenue was significantly higher. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Q2 FY 2022 Results Summary </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Revenue for the second quarter of fiscal 2022 totaled $29.8&nbsp;million, up 8% compared with $27.7&nbsp;million in the year-earlier period. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GAAP gross profit for the second quarter of fiscal 2022 was $12.7&nbsp;million, or 42.6% of revenue, compared with $9.8&nbsp;million, or 35.4% of revenue, in
the same period of fiscal 2021. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> gross profit in the second quarter of fiscal 2022, excluding the CARES Act benefits, was $11.1&nbsp;million, or 37.1% of revenue, up 170 basis points from the gross
profit in the same period of the prior year. The increase compared with the same quarter last year reflects higher revenue and the impact of favorable product mix. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GAAP operating expenses for the second quarter of fiscal 2022 totaled $9.3&nbsp;million, down approximately 3.3% compared with $9.6&nbsp;million in the second
quarter fiscal 2021. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis, excluding the CARES Act benefits, operating expenses for the second quarter of fiscal 2022 were $9.8&nbsp;million, primarily due to higher wages and benefits compared
with the prior-year second quarter, when COVID-related furloughs and work-share programs were in effect.<B> </B> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Other income of $4.3&nbsp;million
included a $4.5&nbsp;million gain, related to the forgiveness indebtedness income related to the PPP loan. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GAAP net income for the second quarter of
fiscal 2022 was $7.0&nbsp;million, or $0.96 per diluted share, compared with net income of $3,000, or $0.00 per diluted share, in the second quarter of fiscal 2021. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis, excluding the CARES Act
benefits, net income for the second quarter of fiscal 2022 was $978,000, or $0.13 per diluted share. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation and
amortization (EBITDA) were $8.7&nbsp;million, compared with $2.4&nbsp;million in the second quarter of fiscal 2021. Second-quarter fiscal 2022 EBITDA, excluding the CARES Act benefits, was $2.1&nbsp;million, or 7.2% of revenue. Adjusted EBITDA was
$9.2&nbsp;million, or 30.8% of revenue, and $2.6&nbsp;million, or 8.7% of revenue, excluding the effect of the CARES Act benefits. This compares with Adjusted EBITDA of $3.0&nbsp;million, or 10.7% of revenue, for the comparable period of fiscal
2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> net income, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> earnings per diluted share, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> gross profit, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating expenses, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> segment operating income, EBITDA, EBITDA excluding the effect of the CARES
Act benefits, Adjusted EBITDA and Adjusted EBITDA excluding the CARES Act benefits are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures explained in greater detail below under &#147;Use of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures.&#148; Please refer to the financial reconciliation table included in this news release for a reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures to the
closest comparable GAAP measures for the fiscal second quarters ended July&nbsp;31, 2021 and August&nbsp;1, 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Bookings for the second quarter of
fiscal 2022 were $30.6&nbsp;million, compared with $25.3&nbsp;million in the second quarter of fiscal 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Backlog at July&nbsp;31, 2021 was
$24.4&nbsp;million versus $23.7&nbsp;million on August&nbsp;1, 2020. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">3 </P>

</DIV></Center>

call, please dial (800) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">437-2398</FONT> (U.S. and Canada) or (929) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">477-0577</FONT> (International) approximately 10 minutes prior to the start time and enter confirmation code
1881865. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">You can hear a replay of the conference call from 12:00 p.m. ET Tuesday, September&nbsp;14, 2021 until 12:00 p.m. ET on Tuesday,
September&nbsp;21, 2021 by dialing (888) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">203-1112</FONT> (U.S. and Canada) or (719) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">457-0820</FONT> (International). The passcode is 1881865. A real-time and an archived audio webcast
of the call will be available through the &#147;Investors&#148; section of the AstroNova website, https://investors.astronovainc.com. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Use of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition to financial measures prepared in accordance with generally accepted
accounting principles (GAAP), this news release contains the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net
income per diluted share, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> gross profit, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating expenses, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> segment operating income, earnings before
interest, taxes, depreciation and amortization (EBITDA), EBITDA excluding the CARES Act benefits, and Adjusted EBITDA and Adjusted EBITDA excluding the CARES Act benefits. AstroNova believes that the inclusion of these
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures helps investors gain a meaningful understanding of changes in the Company&#146;s core operating results, and also can help investors who wish to make comparisons between AstroNova
and other companies on both a GAAP and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis. AstroNova&#146;s management uses these measures, in addition to GAAP financial measures, as the basis for measuring its core operating performance and
comparing such performance to that of prior periods and to the performance of its competitors. These measures also are used by the Company&#146;s management to assist with their financial and operating decision-making. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About AstroNova </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">AstroNova, Inc. (NASDAQ: ALOT), a global
leader in data visualization technologies since 1969, is focused on designing, manufacturing, distributing and servicing a broad range of products that acquire, store, analyze and present data in multiple formats. The Company&#146;s Product
Identification segment offers a complete <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">line-up</FONT> of label and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">direct-to-package</FONT></FONT> printing hardware and supplies, allowing
customers to mark, track and enhance their products&#146; appearance. Supported by AstroNova&#146;s customer application experts and technology leadership in printing, material science and high-speed data processing, customers benefit from an
optimized, &#147;total solution&#148; approach. The Test and Measurement segment includes the AstroNova Aerospace business unit. This segment designs and manufactures flight deck printers, networking hardware and related accessories serving the
world&#146;s aerospace and defense industries with proven advanced airborne technology solutions for the cockpit, the cabin and so much more. AstroNova is a member of the Russell Microcap<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP>
Index and the LD Micro Index (INDEXNYSEGIS: LDMICRO). Additional information is available by visiting www.astronovainc.com.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </P>
